--
-- Name: people; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: colinricardo

CREATE TABLE people (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    name character varying,
    birthdate date,
    deathdate date
);


--
-- Name: people people_pkey; Type: CONSTRAINT; Schema: public; Owner: colinricardo
--

ALTER TABLE ONLY people
    ADD CONSTRAINT people_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id);
